2. When checking in, the staff seemed half asleep (check in at 23:00). When I talked to him, I was really angry at first, but then I felt helpless and wanted to laugh. Forget it, after all, peopleâ€™s professional qualities vary.
3. Half an hour after checking into the room, someone opened the door for no apparent reason. The two people outside the door (who were also check-in personnel) were also confused. As a result, the front desk gave the same room key card.
Regarding the third point, I think the reasons may be as follows:
1. The check-in staff may have felt our anger, so they did it on purpose.
2. There is a problem with the hotel management system. How is it possible to confirm the checked-in room and open it to other people?
This is a problem with both hardware and software.

I originally came here for the Wanda R&F brand. As expected, the facilities are a bit old, which is understandable.

But there are so many problems that make people suspicious. There is no 5-star hardware, but the software (service) is so poor that it has a profound impact.

Of course, this is my first time staying in Wanda, and it will also be my last.
